		// ---------------------------
		// Sporadic case introductions
		// ---------------------------
		
		int ttt = int(t); 	
				
		if (ttt%days_import == 0) {
			
			int impgroup = grp % 2 + 1; 
			grp += 1;
			imptype += 1;
			int stype = imptype%numsubs; 

			if (impgroup == 1) { 
				S_E -= 1; 
				if (stype == 0) { 
					I1_E+= 1; 
				} else if (stype == 1) { 
					I2_E+= 1; 
				} else if (stype == 2) { 
					I3_E+= 1; 
				} 
			}

			if (impgroup == 2) { 
				S_e -= 1; 
				if (stype == 0) { 
					I1_e+= 1; 
				} else if (stype == 1) { 
					I2_e+= 1; 
				} else if (stype == 2) { 
					I3_e+= 1; 
				} 
			}
			
		}
	
		
		
		// ----------------------
		// Differential equations
		// ----------------------
		

		 //dS 
		double dS_E = - eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*S_E/N - eta11*beta_B*(I2_E+II2_E)*S_E/N - eta11*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*S_E/N 
			- eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*S_E/N - eta21*beta_B*(I2_e+II2_e)*S_E/N - eta21*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*S_E/N 
			+ rho*(R48R1_E+R48R2_E+R48R3_E); 
		double dS_e = - eta12*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*S_e/N - eta12*beta_B*(I2_E+II2_E)*S_e/N - eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*S_e/N 
			- eta22*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*S_e/N - eta22*beta_B*(I2_e+II2_e)*S_e/N - eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*S_e/N 
			+ rho*(R48R1_e+R48R2_e+R48R3_e); 

		 //dI 
		double dI1_E = eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*S_E/N + eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*S_E/N
			- h_H1*nu*I1_E - (1-h_H1)*nu*I1_E
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R1R2_E+sigma13*R1R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R1R2_E+sigma13*R1R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R2R2_E+sigma13*R2R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R2R2_E+sigma13*R2R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R3R2_E+sigma13*R3R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R3R2_E+sigma13*R3R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R4R2_E+sigma13*R4R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R4R2_E+sigma13*R4R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R5R2_E+sigma13*R5R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R5R2_E+sigma13*R5R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R6R2_E+sigma13*R6R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R6R2_E+sigma13*R6R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R7R2_E+sigma13*R7R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R7R2_E+sigma13*R7R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R8R2_E+sigma13*R8R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R8R2_E+sigma13*R8R3_E)/N 
			+ eta11*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R9R2_E+sigma13*R9R3_E)/N 
			+ eta21*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*(sigma12*R9R2_E+sigma13*R9R3_E)/N

		double dI1_e = eta12*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*S_e/N + eta22*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*S_e/N
			- h_H1*nu*I1_e - (1-h_H1)*nu*I1_e
			+ eta12*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*(sigma12*R1R2_e+sigma13*R1R3_e)/N

			+ eta21*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R44R1_E+sigma23*R44R2_E)/N

			+ eta21*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R48R1_E+sigma23*R48R2_E)/N; 
		double dJ3_e = eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*S_e/N+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R1R1_e+sigma23*R1R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R2R1_e+sigma23*R2R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R3R1_e+sigma23*R3R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R4R1_e+sigma23*R4R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R5R1_e+sigma23*R5R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R6R1_e+sigma23*R6R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R7R1_e+sigma23*R7R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R8R1_e+sigma23*R8R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R9R1_e+sigma23*R9R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R10R1_e+sigma23*R10R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R11R1_e+sigma23*R11R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R12R1_e+sigma23*R12R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R13R1_e+sigma23*R13R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R14R1_e+sigma23*R14R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R15R1_e+sigma23*R15R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R16R1_e+sigma23*R16R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R17R1_e+sigma23*R17R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R18R1_e+sigma23*R18R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R19R1_e+sigma23*R19R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R20R1_e+sigma23*R20R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R21R1_e+sigma23*R21R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R22R1_e+sigma23*R22R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R23R1_e+sigma23*R23R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R24R1_e+sigma23*R24R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R25R1_e+sigma23*R25R2_e)/N

			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R30R1_e+sigma23*R30R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R31R1_e+sigma23*R31R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R32R1_e+sigma23*R32R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R33R1_e+sigma23*R33R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R34R1_e+sigma23*R34R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R35R1_e+sigma23*R35R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R36R1_e+sigma23*R36R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R37R1_e+sigma23*R37R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R38R1_e+sigma23*R38R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R39R1_e+sigma23*R39R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R40R1_e+sigma23*R40R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R41R1_e+sigma23*R41R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R42R1_e+sigma23*R42R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R43R1_e+sigma23*R43R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R44R1_e+sigma23*R44R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R45R1_e+sigma23*R45R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R46R1_e+sigma23*R46R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R47R1_e+sigma23*R47R2_e)/N 
			+ eta12*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*(sigma13*R48R1_e+sigma23*R48R2_e)/N 
			 + eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*S_e/N+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R1R1_e+sigma23*R1R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R2R1_e+sigma23*R2R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R3R1_e+sigma23*R3R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R4R1_e+sigma23*R4R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R5R1_e+sigma23*R5R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R6R1_e+sigma23*R6R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R7R1_e+sigma23*R7R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R8R1_e+sigma23*R8R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R9R1_e+sigma23*R9R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R10R1_e+sigma23*R10R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R11R1_e+sigma23*R11R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R12R1_e+sigma23*R12R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R13R1_e+sigma23*R13R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R14R1_e+sigma23*R14R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R15R1_e+sigma23*R15R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R16R1_e+sigma23*R16R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R17R1_e+sigma23*R17R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R18R1_e+sigma23*R18R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R19R1_e+sigma23*R19R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R20R1_e+sigma23*R20R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R21R1_e+sigma23*R21R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R22R1_e+sigma23*R22R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R23R1_e+sigma23*R23R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R24R1_e+sigma23*R24R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R25R1_e+sigma23*R25R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R26R1_e+sigma23*R26R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R27R1_e+sigma23*R27R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R28R1_e+sigma23*R28R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R29R1_e+sigma23*R29R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R30R1_e+sigma23*R30R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R31R1_e+sigma23*R31R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R32R1_e+sigma23*R32R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R33R1_e+sigma23*R33R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R34R1_e+sigma23*R34R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R35R1_e+sigma23*R35R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R36R1_e+sigma23*R36R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R37R1_e+sigma23*R37R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R38R1_e+sigma23*R38R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R39R1_e+sigma23*R39R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R40R1_e+sigma23*R40R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R41R1_e+sigma23*R41R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R42R1_e+sigma23*R42R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R43R1_e+sigma23*R43R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R44R1_e+sigma23*R44R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R45R1_e+sigma23*R45R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R46R1_e+sigma23*R46R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R47R1_e+sigma23*R47R2_e)/N 
			+ eta22*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*(sigma13*R48R1_e+sigma23*R48R2_e)/N; 

		 //dII 
		double dII1_E = 
			(1-h_H1)*nu*I1_E - nu*II1_E; 
		double dII1_e = 
			(1-h_H1)*nu*I1_e - nu*II1_e; 
		double dII2_E = 
			(1-h_B)*nu*I2_E - nu*II2_E; 
		double dII2_e = 
			(1-h_B)*nu*I2_e - nu*II2_e; 
		double dII3_E = 
			(1-h_H3)*nu*I3_E - nu*II3_E; 
		double dII3_e = 
			(1-h_H3)*nu*I3_e - nu*II3_e; 

		 //dH 
		double dH1_E = h_H1*nu*I1_E - d_H1*nu*H1_E - (1-d_H1)*nu*H1_E; 
		double dH1_e = h_H1*nu*I1_e - d_H1*nu*H1_e - (1-d_H1)*nu*H1_e; 
		double dH2_E = h_B*nu*I2_E - d_B*nu*H2_E - (1-d_B)*nu*H2_E; 
		double dH2_e = h_B*nu*I2_e - d_B*nu*H2_e - (1-d_B)*nu*H2_e; 
		double dH3_E = h_H3*nu*I3_E - d_H3*nu*H3_E - (1-d_H3)*nu*H3_E; 
		double dH3_e = h_H3*nu*I3_e - d_H3*nu*H3_e - (1-d_H3)*nu*H3_e; 

		 //d R 1 R  
		double dR1R1_E = nu*II1_E + (1-d_H1)*nu*H1_E
			- eta11*sigma12*beta_B*(I2_E+II2_E)*R1R1_E/N - eta11*sigma13*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*R1R1_E/N
			- eta21*sigma12*beta_B*(I2_e+II2_e)*R1R1_E/N - eta21*sigma13*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*R1R1_E/N
			- rho*R1R1_E; 
		double dR1R1_e = nu*II1_e + (1-d_H1)*nu*H1_e
			- eta12*sigma12*beta_B*(I2_E+II2_E)*R1R1_e/N - eta12*sigma13*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*R1R1_e/N
			- eta22*sigma12*beta_B*(I2_e+II2_e)*R1R1_e/N - eta22*sigma13*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*R1R1_e/N
			- rho*R1R1_e; 
		double dR1R2_E = nu*II2_E + (1-d_B)*nu*H2_E
			- eta11*sigma12*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*R1R2_E/N - eta11*sigma23*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*R1R2_E/N
			- eta21*sigma12*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*R1R2_E/N - eta21*sigma23*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*R1R2_E/N
			- rho*R1R2_E; 
		double dR1R2_e = nu*II2_e + (1-d_B)*nu*H2_e
			- eta12*sigma12*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*R1R2_e/N - eta12*sigma23*beta_H3*(I3_E+II3_E)*R1R2_e/N
			- eta22*sigma12*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*R1R2_e/N - eta22*sigma23*beta_H3*(I3_e+II3_e)*R1R2_e/N
			- rho*R1R2_e; 
		double dR1R3_E = nu*II3_E + (1-d_H3)*nu*H3_E
			- eta11*sigma13*beta_H1*(I1_E+II1_E)*R1R3_E/N - eta11*sigma23*beta_B*(I2_E+II2_E)*R1R3_E/N
			- eta21*sigma13*beta_H1*(I1_e+II1_e)*R1R3_E/N - eta21*sigma23*beta_B*(I2_e+II2_e)*R1R3_E/N
			- rho*R1R3_E;

		double dD = d_H1*nu*H1_E + d_B*nu*H2_E + d_H3*nu*H3_E +

		// -----------------
		// Birth/death/aging
		// -----------------
	
		dS_E +=  - 0.03835616*S_E/1000;
		dI1_E +=  - 0.03835616*I1_E/1000;
		dI2_E +=  - 0.03835616*I2_E/1000;
		dI3_E +=  - 0.03835616*I3_E/1000;
		dII1_E +=  - 0.03835616*II1_E/1000;
		dII2_E +=  - 0.03835616*II2_E/1000;
		dII3_E +=  - 0.03835616*II3_E/1000;
		dH1_E +=  - 0.03835616*H1_E/1000;
		dH2_E +=  - 0.03835616*H2_E/1000;
		dH3_E +=  - 0.03835616*H3_E/1000;
		dR1R1_E +=  - 0.03835616*R1R1_E/1000;
		dR1R2_E +=  - 0.03835616*R1R2_E/1000;
		dR1R3_E +=  - 0.03835616*R1R3_E/1000;
		dR2R1_E +=  - 0.03835616*R2R1_E/1000;
		dR2R2_E +=  - 0.03835616*R2R2_E/1000;
		dR2R3_E +=  - 0.03835616*R2R3_E/1000;
		dR3R1_E +=  - 0.03835616*R3R1_E/1000;
		dR3R2_E +=  - 0.03835616*R3R2_E/1000;
		dR3R3_E +=  - 0.03835616*R3R3_E/1000;
		dR4R1_E +=  - 0.03835616*R4R1_E/1000;
